\DoxyCodeLine{00243\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00244\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ Henceforth\ the\ source\ version\ will\ match\ the\ shared-\/library\ major\ and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00245\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ minor\ numbers;\ the\ shared-\/library\ major\ version\ number\ will\ be\ used\ for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00246\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ changes\ in\ backward\ compatibility,\ as\ it\ is\ intended.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00247\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ The\ PNG\_LIBPNG\_VER\ macro,\ which\ is\ not\ used\ within\ libpng\ but\ is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00248\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ available\ for\ applications,\ is\ an\ unsigned\ integer\ of\ the\ form\ XYYZZ}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00249\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ corresponding\ to\ the\ source\ version\ X.Y.Z\ (leading\ zeros\ in\ Y\ and\ Z).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00250\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ Beta\ versions\ were\ given\ the\ previous\ public\ release\ number\ plus\ a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00251\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ letter,\ until\ version\ 1.0.6j;\ from\ then\ on\ they\ were\ given\ the\ upcoming}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00252\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ public\ release\ number\ plus\ "{}betaNN"{}\ or\ "{}rcNN"{}.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00253\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00254\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ Binary\ incompatibility\ exists\ only\ when\ applications\ make\ direct\ access}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00255\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ to\ the\ info\_ptr\ or\ png\_ptr\ members\ through\ png.h,\ and\ the\ compiled}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00256\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ application\ is\ loaded\ with\ a\ different\ version\ of\ the\ library.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00257\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00258\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ DLLNUM\ will\ change\ each\ time\ there\ are\ forward\ or\ backward\ changes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00259\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ in\ binary\ compatibility\ (e.g.,\ when\ a\ new\ feature\ is\ added).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00260\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00261\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ See\ libpng.txt\ or\ libpng.3\ for\ more\ information.\ \ The\ PNG\ specification}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00262\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ is\ available\ as\ a\ W3C\ Recommendation\ and\ as\ an\ ISO/IEC\ Standard;\ see}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00391\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ Section\ 1:\ [omitted]\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00392\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00393\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ Section\ 2:\ run\ time\ configuration}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00394\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ See\ pnglibconf.h\ for\ build\ time\ configuration}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00395\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00396\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Run\ time\ configuration\ allows\ the\ application\ to\ choose\ between}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00397\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ implementations\ of\ certain\ arithmetic\ APIs.\ \ The\ default\ is\ set}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00398\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ at\ build\ time\ and\ recorded\ in\ pnglibconf.h,\ but\ it\ is\ safe\ to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00399\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ override\ these\ (and\ only\ these)\ settings.\ \ Note\ that\ this\ won't}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00400\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ change\ what\ the\ library\ does,\ only\ application\ code,\ and\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00401\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ settings\ can\ (and\ probably\ should)\ be\ made\ on\ a\ per-\/file\ basis}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00402\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ by\ setting\ the\ \#defines\ before\ including\ png.h}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00403\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00404\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Use\ macros\ to\ read\ integers\ from\ PNG\ data\ or\ use\ the\ exported}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00405\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ functions?}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00406\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ PNG\_USE\_READ\_MACROS:\ use\ the\ macros\ (see\ below)\ \ Note\ that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00407\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ the\ macros\ evaluate\ their\ argument\ multiple\ times.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00408\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ PNG\_NO\_USE\_READ\_MACROS:\ call\ the\ relevant\ library\ function.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00409\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00410\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Use\ the\ alternative\ algorithm\ for\ compositing\ alpha\ samples\ that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00411\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ does\ not\ use\ division?}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00412\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ PNG\_READ\_COMPOSITE\_NODIV\_SUPPORTED:\ use\ the\ 'no\ division'}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00413\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ algorithm.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00414\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ PNG\_NO\_READ\_COMPOSITE\_NODIV:\ use\ the\ 'division'\ algorithm.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00415\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00416\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ How\ to\ handle\ benign\ errors\ if\ PNG\_ALLOW\_BENIGN\_ERRORS\ is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00417\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ false?}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00418\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ PNG\_ALLOW\_BENIGN\_ERRORS:\ map\ calls\ to\ the\ benign\ error}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00419\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ APIs\ to\ png\_warning.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00420\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Otherwise\ the\ calls\ are\ mapped\ to\ png\_error.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00421\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00422\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00423\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ Section\ 3:\ type\ definitions,\ including\ structures\ and\ compile\ time}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00424\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ constants.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00425\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ See\ pngconf.h\ for\ base\ types\ that\ vary\ by\ machine/system}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00426\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00427\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00428\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ This\ triggers\ a\ compiler\ error\ in\ png.c,\ if\ png.c\ and\ png.h}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00429\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ do\ not\ agree\ upon\ the\ version\ number.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00430\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00431\ \textcolor{keyword}{typedef}\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}*\ \mbox{\hyperlink{libpng16_2png_8h_a4bb9a5c9a50ab5ce8037342158a2ad23}{png\_libpng\_version\_1\_6\_39}};}
\DoxyCodeLine{00432\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00433\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ Basic\ control\ structions.\ \ Read\ libpng-\/manual.txt\ or\ libpng.3\ for\ more\ info.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00434\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00435\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ png\_struct\ is\ the\ cache\ of\ information\ used\ while\ reading\ or\ writing\ a\ single}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00436\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ PNG\ file.\ \ One\ of\ these\ is\ always\ required,\ although\ the\ simplified\ API}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00437\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ (below)\ hides\ the\ creation\ and\ destruction\ of\ it.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00444\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ png\_info\ contains\ information\ read\ from\ or\ to\ be\ written\ to\ a\ PNG\ file.\ \ One}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00448\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ information\ during\ read\ and\ "{}png\_set\_"{}\ functions\ calls\ write\ information}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00449\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ when\ creating\ a\ PNG.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00450\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ been\ moved\ into\ a\ separate\ header\ file\ that\ is\ not\ accessible\ to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00451\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ applications.\ \ Read\ libpng-\/manual.txt\ or\ libpng.3\ for\ more\ info.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00458\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ Types\ with\ names\ ending\ 'p'\ are\ pointer\ types.\ \ The\ corresponding\ types\ with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00459\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ names\ ending\ 'rp'\ are\ identical\ pointer\ types\ except\ that\ the\ pointer\ is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00460\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ marked\ 'restrict',\ which\ means\ that\ it\ is\ the\ only\ pointer\ to\ the\ object}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00461\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ passed\ to\ the\ function.\ \ Applications\ should\ not\ use\ the\ 'restrict'\ types;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00462\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ it\ is\ always\ valid\ to\ pass\ 'p'\ to\ a\ pointer\ with\ a\ function\ argument\ of\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00463\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ corresponding\ 'rp'\ type.\ \ Different\ compilers\ have\ different\ rules\ with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00464\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ regard\ to\ type\ matching\ in\ the\ presence\ of\ 'restrict'.\ \ For\ backward}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00465\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ compatibility\ libpng\ callbacks\ never\ have\ 'restrict'\ in\ their\ parameters\ and,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00466\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ consequentially,\ writing\ portable\ application\ code\ is\ extremely\ difficult\ if}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00467\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ an\ attempt\ is\ made\ to\ use\ 'restrict'.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00468\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00469\ \textcolor{keyword}{typedef}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{libpng16_2png_8h_a27de3cfa4c573aab4f4af60ce6325607}{png\_struct}}\ *\ \mbox{\hyperlink{libpng16_2pngconf_8h_af21b002e402fd844f1767dc3e7e92756}{PNG\_RESTRICT}}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{libpng16_2png_8h_afd0519b307fc9e36f645ad6eaf620d05}{png\_structrp}};}

\DoxyCodeLine{00544\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifdef\ PNG\_TEXT\_SUPPORTED}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00545\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ png\_text\ holds\ the\ contents\ of\ a\ text/ztxt/itxt\ chunk\ in\ a\ PNG\ file,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00546\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ and\ whether\ that\ contents\ is\ compressed\ or\ not.\ \ The\ "{}key"{}\ field}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00547\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ points\ to\ a\ regular\ zero-\/terminated\ C\ string.\ \ The\ "{}text"{}\ fields\ can\ be\ a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00548\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ regular\ C\ string,\ an\ empty\ string,\ or\ a\ NULL\ pointer.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00549\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ However,\ the\ structure\ returned\ by\ png\_get\_text()\ will\ always\ contain}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00550\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ the\ "{}text"{}\ field\ as\ a\ regular\ zero-\/terminated\ C\ string\ (possibly}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00551\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ empty),\ never\ a\ NULL\ pointer,\ so\ it\ can\ be\ safely\ used\ in\ printf()\ and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00552\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ other\ string-\/handling\ functions.\ \ Note\ that\ the\ "{}itxt\_length"{},\ "{}lang"{},\ and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00553\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ "{}lang\_key"{}\ members\ of\ the\ structure\ only\ exist\ when\ the\ library\ is\ built}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00554\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ with\ iTXt\ chunk\ support.\ \ Prior\ to\ libpng-\/1.4.0\ the\ library\ was\ built\ by}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00555\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ default\ without\ iTXt\ support.\ Also\ note\ that\ when\ iTXt\ *is*\ supported,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00556\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ the\ "{}lang"{}\ and\ "{}lang\_key"{}\ fields\ contain\ NULL\ pointers\ when\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00557\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ "{}compression"{}\ field\ contains\ *\ PNG\_TEXT\_COMPRESSION\_NONE\ or}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00558\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ PNG\_TEXT\_COMPRESSION\_zTXt.\ Note\ that\ the\ "{}compression\ value"{}\ is\ not\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00559\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ same\ as\ what\ appears\ in\ the\ PNG\ tEXt/zTXt/iTXt\ chunk's\ "{}compression\ flag"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00560\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ which\ is\ always\ 0\ or\ 1,\ or\ its\ "{}compression\ method"{}\ which\ is\ always\ 0.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00561\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00871\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ Section\ 4:\ exported\ functions}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00872\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Here\ are\ the\ function\ definitions\ most\ commonly\ used.\ \ This\ is\ not}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00873\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ the\ place\ to\ find\ out\ how\ to\ use\ libpng.\ \ See\ libpng-\/manual.txt\ for\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00874\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ full\ explanation,\ see\ example.c\ for\ the\ summary.\ \ This\ just\ provides}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00875\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ a\ simple\ one\ line\ description\ of\ the\ use\ of\ each\ function.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00876\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00877\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ The\ PNG\_EXPORT()\ and\ PNG\_EXPORTA()\ macros\ used\ below\ are\ defined\ in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00878\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ pngconf.h\ and\ in\ the\ *.dfn\ files\ in\ the\ scripts\ directory.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00879\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00880\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ PNG\_EXPORT(ordinal,\ type,\ name,\ (args));}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00881\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00882\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ ordinal:\ \ \ \ ordinal\ that\ is\ used\ while\ building}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00883\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ *.def\ files.\ The\ ordinal\ value\ is\ only}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00884\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ relevant\ when\ preprocessing\ png.h\ with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00885\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ the\ *.dfn\ files\ for\ building\ symbol\ table}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00886\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ entries,\ and\ are\ removed\ by\ pngconf.h.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00887\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ type:\ \ \ \ \ \ \ return\ type\ of\ the\ function}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00888\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ name:\ \ \ \ \ \ \ function\ name}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00889\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ args:\ \ \ \ \ \ \ function\ arguments,\ with\ types}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00890\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00891\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ When\ we\ wish\ to\ append\ attributes\ to\ a\ function\ prototype\ we\ use}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00892\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ the\ PNG\_EXPORTA()\ macro\ instead.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00893\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00894\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ PNG\_EXPORTA(ordinal,\ type,\ name,\ (args),\ attributes);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00895\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00896\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ ordinal,\ type,\ name,\ and\ args:\ same\ as\ in\ PNG\_EXPORT().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00897\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ attributes:\ function\ attributes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00898\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00899\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00900\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ Returns\ the\ version\ number\ of\ the\ library\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00901\ \mbox{\hyperlink{libpng16_2pngconf_8h_abbd10d3d08ec9421a5d1792c72568fbe}{PNG\_EXPORT}}(1,\ \mbox{\hyperlink{libpng16_2pngconf_8h_a3f5733db02bc80832c61c24b76d21bfc}{png\_uint\_32}},\ png\_access\_version\_number,\ (\textcolor{keywordtype}{void}));}
\DoxyCodeLine{00902\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00903\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ Tell\ lib\ we\ have\ already\ handled\ the\ first\ <num\_bytes>\ magic\ bytes.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00904\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Handling\ more\ than\ 8\ bytes\ from\ the\ beginning\ of\ the\ file\ is\ an\ error.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{01095\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifdef\ PNG\_READ\_ALPHA\_MODE\_SUPPORTED}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01096\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ How\ the\ alpha\ channel\ is\ interpreted\ -\/\ this\ affects\ how\ the\ color\ channels}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01097\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ of\ a\ PNG\ file\ are\ returned\ to\ the\ calling\ application\ when\ an\ alpha\ channel,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01098\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ or\ a\ tRNS\ chunk\ in\ a\ palette\ file,\ is\ present.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01099\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01100\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ This\ has\ no\ effect\ on\ the\ way\ pixels\ are\ written\ into\ a\ PNG\ output}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01101\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ datastream.\ The\ color\ samples\ in\ a\ PNG\ datastream\ are\ never\ premultiplied}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01102\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ with\ the\ alpha\ samples.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01103\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01104\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ The\ default\ is\ to\ return\ data\ according\ to\ the\ PNG\ specification:\ the\ alpha}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01105\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ channel\ is\ a\ linear\ measure\ of\ the\ contribution\ of\ the\ pixel\ to\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01106\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ corresponding\ composited\ pixel,\ and\ the\ color\ channels\ are\ unassociated}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01107\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ (not\ premultiplied).\ \ The\ gamma\ encoded\ color\ channels\ must\ be\ scaled}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01108\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ according\ to\ the\ contribution\ and\ to\ do\ this\ it\ is\ necessary\ to\ undo}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01109\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ the\ encoding,\ scale\ the\ color\ values,\ perform\ the\ composition\ and\ re-\/encode}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01110\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ the\ values.\ \ This\ is\ the\ 'PNG'\ mode.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01111\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01112\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ The\ alternative\ is\ to\ 'associate'\ the\ alpha\ with\ the\ color\ information\ by}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01113\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ storing\ color\ channel\ values\ that\ have\ been\ scaled\ by\ the\ alpha.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01114\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ image.\ \ These\ are\ the\ 'STANDARD',\ 'ASSOCIATED'\ or\ 'PREMULTIPLIED'\ modes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01115\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ (the\ latter\ being\ the\ two\ common\ names\ for\ associated\ alpha\ color\ channels).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01116\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01117\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ For\ the\ 'OPTIMIZED'\ mode,\ a\ pixel\ is\ treated\ as\ opaque\ only\ if\ the\ alpha}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01118\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ value\ is\ equal\ to\ the\ maximum\ value.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01119\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01120\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ The\ final\ choice\ is\ to\ gamma\ encode\ the\ alpha\ channel\ as\ well.\ \ This\ is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01121\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ broken\ because,\ in\ practice,\ no\ implementation\ that\ uses\ this\ choice}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01122\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ correctly\ undoes\ the\ encoding\ before\ handling\ alpha\ composition.\ \ Use\ this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01123\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ choice\ only\ if\ other\ serious\ errors\ in\ the\ software\ or\ hardware\ you\ use}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01124\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ mandate\ it;\ the\ typical\ serious\ error\ is\ for\ dark\ halos\ to\ appear\ around}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01125\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ opaque\ areas\ of\ the\ composited\ PNG\ image\ because\ of\ arithmetic\ overflow.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01126\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01127\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ The\ API\ function\ png\_set\_alpha\_mode\ specifies\ which\ of\ these\ choices\ to\ use}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01128\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ with\ an\ enumerated\ 'mode'\ value\ and\ the\ gamma\ of\ the\ required\ output:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01129\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01130\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define\ PNG\_ALPHA\_PNG\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ 0\ }\textcolor{comment}{/*\ according\ to\ the\ PNG\ standard\ */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01131\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define\ PNG\_ALPHA\_STANDARD\ \ \ \ \ \ 1\ }\textcolor{comment}{/*\ according\ to\ Porter/Duff\ */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01132\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define\ PNG\_ALPHA\_ASSOCIATED\ \ \ \ 1\ }\textcolor{comment}{/*\ as\ above;\ this\ is\ the\ normal\ practice\ */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01133\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define\ PNG\_ALPHA\_PREMULTIPLIED\ 1\ }\textcolor{comment}{/*\ as\ above\ */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01134\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define\ PNG\_ALPHA\_OPTIMIZED\ \ \ \ \ 2\ }\textcolor{comment}{/*\ 'PNG'\ for\ opaque\ pixels,\ else\ 'STANDARD'\ */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01135\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define\ PNG\_ALPHA\_BROKEN\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ 3\ }\textcolor{comment}{/*\ the\ alpha\ channel\ is\ gamma\ encoded\ */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01136\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{01137\ \mbox{\hyperlink{libpng16_2pngconf_8h_ab4862d69c446ce9b210ebbecf54f368d}{PNG\_FP\_EXPORT}}(227,\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{void},\ png\_set\_alpha\_mode,\ (\mbox{\hyperlink{libpng16_2png_8h_afd0519b307fc9e36f645ad6eaf620d05}{png\_structrp}}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{libpng16_2png_8h_a35dc82857793b55e7c8bb6f32f8ca764}{png\_ptr}},\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui__impl__opengl3__loader_8h_a1e71d9c196e4683cc06c4b54d53f7ef5}{mode}},}

\DoxyCodeLine{01143\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if\ defined(PNG\_GAMMA\_SUPPORTED)\ ||\ defined(PNG\_READ\_ALPHA\_MODE\_SUPPORTED)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01144\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ The\ output\_gamma\ value\ is\ a\ screen\ gamma\ in\ libpng\ terminology:\ it\ expresses}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01145\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ how\ to\ decode\ the\ output\ values,\ not\ how\ they\ are\ encoded.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01146\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{01152\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{01153\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ The\ following\ are\ examples\ of\ calls\ to\ png\_set\_alpha\_mode\ to\ achieve\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01154\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ required\ overall\ gamma\ correction\ and,\ where\ necessary,\ alpha}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01155\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ premultiplication.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01156\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01157\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ png\_set\_alpha\_mode(pp,\ PNG\_ALPHA\_PNG,\ PNG\_DEFAULT\_sRGB);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01158\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ This\ is\ the\ default\ libpng\ handling\ of\ the\ alpha\ channel\ -\/\ it\ is\ not}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01159\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ pre-\/multiplied\ into\ the\ color\ components.\ \ In\ addition\ the\ call\ states}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01160\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ that\ the\ output\ is\ for\ a\ sRGB\ system\ and\ causes\ all\ PNG\ files\ without\ gAMA}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01161\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ chunks\ to\ be\ assumed\ to\ be\ encoded\ using\ sRGB.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01162\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01163\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ png\_set\_alpha\_mode(pp,\ PNG\_ALPHA\_PNG,\ PNG\_GAMMA\_MAC);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01164\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ In\ this\ case\ the\ output\ is\ assumed\ to\ be\ something\ like\ an\ sRGB\ conformant}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01165\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ display\ preceded\ by\ a\ power-\/law\ lookup\ table\ of\ power\ 1.45.\ \ This\ is\ how}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01166\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ early\ Mac\ systems\ behaved.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01167\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01168\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ png\_set\_alpha\_mode(pp,\ PNG\_ALPHA\_STANDARD,\ PNG\_GAMMA\_LINEAR);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01169\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ This\ is\ the\ classic\ Jim\ Blinn\ approach\ and\ will\ work\ in\ academic}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01170\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ environments\ where\ everything\ is\ done\ by\ the\ book.\ \ It\ has\ the\ shortcoming}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01171\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ of\ assuming\ that\ input\ PNG\ data\ with\ no\ gamma\ information\ is\ linear\ -\/\ this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01172\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ is\ unlikely\ to\ be\ correct\ unless\ the\ PNG\ files\ where\ generated\ locally.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01173\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ Most\ of\ the\ time\ the\ output\ precision\ will\ be\ so\ low\ as\ to\ show}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01174\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ significant\ banding\ in\ dark\ areas\ of\ the\ image.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01175\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01176\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ png\_set\_expand\_16(pp);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01177\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ png\_set\_alpha\_mode(pp,\ PNG\_ALPHA\_STANDARD,\ PNG\_DEFAULT\_sRGB);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01178\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ This\ is\ a\ somewhat\ more\ realistic\ Jim\ Blinn\ inspired\ approach.\ \ PNG\ files}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01179\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ are\ assumed\ to\ have\ the\ sRGB\ encoding\ if\ not\ marked\ with\ a\ gamma\ value\ and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01180\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ the\ output\ is\ always\ 16\ bits\ per\ component.\ \ This\ permits\ accurate\ scaling}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01181\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ and\ processing\ of\ the\ data.\ \ If\ you\ know\ that\ your\ input\ PNG\ files\ were}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01182\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ generated\ locally\ you\ might\ need\ to\ replace\ PNG\_DEFAULT\_sRGB\ with\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01183\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ correct\ value\ for\ your\ system.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01184\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01185\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ png\_set\_alpha\_mode(pp,\ PNG\_ALPHA\_OPTIMIZED,\ PNG\_DEFAULT\_sRGB);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01186\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ If\ you\ just\ need\ to\ composite\ the\ PNG\ image\ onto\ an\ existing\ background}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01187\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ and\ if\ you\ control\ the\ code\ that\ does\ this\ you\ can\ use\ the\ optimization}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01188\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ setting.\ \ In\ this\ case\ you\ just\ copy\ completely\ opaque\ pixels\ to\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01189\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ output.\ \ For\ pixels\ that\ are\ not\ completely\ transparent\ (you\ just\ skip}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01190\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ those)\ you\ do\ the\ composition\ math\ using\ png\_composite\ or\ png\_composite\_16}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01191\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ below\ then\ encode\ the\ resultant\ 8-\/bit\ or\ 16-\/bit\ values\ to\ match\ the\ output}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01192\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ encoding.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01193\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01194\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Other\ cases}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01195\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ If\ neither\ the\ PNG\ nor\ the\ standard\ linear\ encoding\ work\ for\ you\ because}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01196\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ of\ the\ software\ or\ hardware\ you\ use\ then\ you\ have\ a\ big\ problem.\ \ The\ PNG}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01197\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ case\ will\ probably\ result\ in\ halos\ around\ the\ image.\ \ The\ linear\ encoding}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01198\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ will\ probably\ result\ in\ a\ washed\ out,\ too\ bright,\ image\ (it's\ actually\ too}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01199\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ contrasty.)\ \ Try\ the\ ALPHA\_OPTIMIZED\ mode\ above\ -\/\ this\ will\ probably}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01200\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ substantially\ reduce\ the\ halos.\ \ Alternatively\ try:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01201\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01202\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ png\_set\_alpha\_mode(pp,\ PNG\_ALPHA\_BROKEN,\ PNG\_DEFAULT\_sRGB);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01203\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ This\ option\ will\ also\ reduce\ the\ halos,\ but\ there\ will\ be\ slight\ dark}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01204\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ halos\ round\ the\ opaque\ parts\ of\ the\ image\ where\ the\ background\ is\ light.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01205\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ In\ the\ OPTIMIZED\ mode\ the\ halos\ will\ be\ light\ halos\ where\ the\ background}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01206\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ is\ dark.\ \ Take\ your\ pick\ -\/\ the\ halos\ are\ unavoidable\ unless\ you\ can\ get}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01207\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ your\ hardware/software\ fixed!\ \ (The\ OPTIMIZED\ approach\ is\ slightly}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01208\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ faster.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01209\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01210\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ When\ the\ default\ gamma\ of\ PNG\ files\ doesn't\ match\ the\ output\ gamma.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01211\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ If\ you\ have\ PNG\ files\ with\ no\ gamma\ information\ png\_set\_alpha\_mode\ allows}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01212\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ you\ to\ provide\ a\ default\ gamma,\ but\ it\ also\ sets\ the\ output\ gamma\ to\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01213\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ matching\ value.\ \ If\ you\ know\ your\ PNG\ files\ have\ a\ gamma\ that\ doesn't}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01214\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ match\ the\ output\ you\ can\ take\ advantage\ of\ the\ fact\ that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01215\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ png\_set\_alpha\_mode\ always\ sets\ the\ output\ gamma\ but\ only\ sets\ the\ PNG}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01216\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ default\ if\ it\ is\ not\ already\ set:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01217\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01218\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ png\_set\_alpha\_mode(pp,\ PNG\_ALPHA\_PNG,\ PNG\_DEFAULT\_sRGB);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01219\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ png\_set\_alpha\_mode(pp,\ PNG\_ALPHA\_PNG,\ PNG\_GAMMA\_MAC);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01220\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ The\ first\ call\ sets\ both\ the\ default\ and\ the\ output\ gamma\ values,\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01221\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ second\ call\ overrides\ the\ output\ gamma\ without\ changing\ the\ default.\ \ This}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01222\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ is\ easier\ than\ achieving\ the\ same\ effect\ with\ png\_set\_gamma.\ \ You\ must\ use}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01223\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ PNG\_ALPHA\_PNG\ for\ the\ first\ call\ -\/\ internal\ checking\ in\ png\_set\_alpha\ will}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01224\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ fire\ if\ more\ than\ one\ call\ to\ png\_set\_alpha\_mode\ and\ png\_set\_background\ is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01225\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ made\ in\ the\ same\ read\ operation,\ however\ multiple\ calls\ with\ PNG\_ALPHA\_PNG}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01226\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ are\ ignored.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01227\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{01652\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01653\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ There\ is\ no\ write\ support\ -\/\ on\ write,\ by\ default,\ all\ the\ chunks\ in\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01654\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ 'unknown'\ list\ are\ written\ in\ the\ specified\ position.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01655\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}

\DoxyCodeLine{01657\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01658\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ negative:\ An\ error\ occurred;\ png\_chunk\_error\ will\ be\ called.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01659\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ zero:\ The\ chunk\ was\ not\ handled,\ the\ chunk\ will\ be\ saved.\ A\ critical}}

\DoxyCodeLine{01661\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ positive:\ The\ chunk\ was\ handled,\ libpng\ will\ ignore/discard\ it.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01662\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02177\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif\ }\textcolor{comment}{/*\ sCAL\ */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02178\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{02179\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifdef\ PNG\_SET\_UNKNOWN\_CHUNKS\_SUPPORTED}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02180\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ Provide\ the\ default\ handling\ for\ all\ unknown\ chunks\ or,\ optionally,\ for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02181\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ specific\ unknown\ chunks.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02182\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02183\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ NOTE:\ prior\ to\ 1.6.0\ the\ handling\ specified\ for\ particular\ chunks\ on\ read\ was}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02184\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ ignored\ and\ the\ default\ was\ used,\ the\ per-\/chunk\ setting\ only\ had\ an\ effect\ on}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02185\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ write.\ \ If\ you\ wish\ to\ have\ chunk-\/specific\ handling\ on\ read\ in\ code\ that\ must}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02186\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ work\ on\ earlier\ versions\ you\ must\ use\ a\ user\ chunk\ callback\ to\ specify\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02187\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ desired\ handling\ (keep\ or\ discard.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02188\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02189\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ The\ 'keep'\ parameter\ is\ a\ PNG\_HANDLE\_CHUNK\_\ value\ as\ listed\ below.\ \ The}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02190\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ parameter\ is\ interpreted\ as\ follows:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02191\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02192\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ READ:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02193\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ PNG\_HANDLE\_CHUNK\_AS\_DEFAULT:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02194\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ Known\ chunks:\ do\ normal\ libpng\ processing,\ do\ not\ keep\ the\ chunk\ (but}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02195\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ see\ the\ comments\ below\ about\ PNG\_HANDLE\_AS\_UNKNOWN\_SUPPORTED)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02196\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ Unknown\ chunks:\ for\ a\ specific\ chunk\ use\ the\ global\ default,\ when\ used}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02197\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ as\ the\ default\ discard\ the\ chunk\ data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02198\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ PNG\_HANDLE\_CHUNK\_NEVER:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02199\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ Discard\ the\ chunk\ data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02200\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ PNG\_HANDLE\_CHUNK\_IF\_SAFE:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02201\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ Keep\ the\ chunk\ data\ if\ the\ chunk\ is\ not\ critical\ else\ raise\ a\ chunk}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02202\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ error.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02203\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ PNG\_HANDLE\_CHUNK\_ALWAYS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02204\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ Keep\ the\ chunk\ data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02205\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02206\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ If\ the\ chunk\ data\ is\ saved\ it\ can\ be\ retrieved\ using\ png\_get\_unknown\_chunks,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02207\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ below.\ \ Notice\ that\ specifying\ "{}AS\_DEFAULT"{}\ as\ a\ global\ default\ is\ equivalent}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02208\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ to\ specifying\ "{}NEVER"{},\ however\ when\ "{}AS\_DEFAULT"{}\ is\ used\ for\ specific\ chunks}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02209\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ it\ simply\ resets\ the\ behavior\ to\ the\ libpng\ default.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02210\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02211\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ INTERACTION\ WITH\ USER\ CHUNK\ CALLBACKS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02212\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ The\ per-\/chunk\ handling\ is\ always\ used\ when\ there\ is\ a\ png\_user\_chunk\_ptr}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02213\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ callback\ and\ the\ callback\ returns\ 0;\ the\ chunk\ is\ then\ always\ stored\ *unless*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02214\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ it\ is\ critical\ and\ the\ per-\/chunk\ setting\ is\ other\ than\ ALWAYS.\ \ Notice\ that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02215\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ the\ global\ default\ is\ *not*\ used\ in\ this\ case.\ \ (In\ effect\ the\ per-\/chunk}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02216\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ value\ is\ incremented\ to\ at\ least\ IF\_SAFE.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02217\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02218\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ IMPORTANT\ NOTE:\ this\ behavior\ will\ change\ in\ libpng\ 1.7\ -\/\ the\ global\ and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02219\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ per-\/chunk\ defaults\ will\ be\ honored.\ \ If\ you\ want\ to\ preserve\ the\ current}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02220\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ behavior\ when\ your\ callback\ returns\ 0\ you\ must\ set\ PNG\_HANDLE\_CHUNK\_IF\_SAFE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02221\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ as\ the\ default\ -\/\ if\ you\ don't\ do\ this\ libpng\ 1.6\ will\ issue\ a\ warning.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02222\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02223\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ If\ you\ want\ unhandled\ unknown\ chunks\ to\ be\ discarded\ in\ libpng\ 1.6\ and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02224\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ earlier\ simply\ return\ '1'\ (handled).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02225\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02226\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ PNG\_HANDLE\_AS\_UNKNOWN\_SUPPORTED:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02227\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ If\ this\ is\ *not*\ set\ known\ chunks\ will\ always\ be\ handled\ by\ libpng\ and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02228\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ will\ never\ be\ stored\ in\ the\ unknown\ chunk\ list.\ \ Known\ chunks\ listed\ to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02229\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ png\_set\_keep\_unknown\_chunks\ will\ have\ no\ effect.\ \ If\ it\ is\ set\ then\ known}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02230\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ chunks\ listed\ with\ a\ keep\ other\ than\ AS\_DEFAULT\ will\ *never*\ be\ processed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02231\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ by\ libpng,\ in\ addition\ critical\ chunks\ must\ either\ be\ processed\ by\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02232\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ callback\ or\ saved.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02233\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02234\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ The\ IHDR\ and\ IEND\ chunks\ must\ not\ be\ listed.\ \ Because\ this\ turns\ off\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02235\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ default\ handling\ for\ chunks\ that\ would\ otherwise\ be\ recognized\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02236\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ behavior\ of\ libpng\ transformations\ may\ well\ become\ incorrect!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02237\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02238\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ WRITE:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02239\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ When\ writing\ chunks\ the\ options\ only\ apply\ to\ the\ chunks\ specified\ by}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02240\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ png\_set\_unknown\_chunks\ (below),\ libpng\ will\ *always*\ write\ known\ chunks}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02241\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ required\ by\ png\_set\_\ calls\ and\ will\ always\ write\ the\ core\ critical\ chunks}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02242\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ (as\ required\ for\ PLTE).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02243\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02244\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ Each\ chunk\ in\ the\ png\_set\_unknown\_chunks\ list\ is\ looked\ up\ in\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02245\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ png\_set\_keep\_unknown\_chunks\ list\ to\ find\ the\ keep\ setting,\ this\ is\ then}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02246\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ interpreted\ as\ follows:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02247\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02248\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ PNG\_HANDLE\_CHUNK\_AS\_DEFAULT:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02249\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ Write\ safe-\/to-\/copy\ chunks\ and\ write\ other\ chunks\ if\ the\ global}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02250\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ default\ is\ set\ to\ \_ALWAYS,\ otherwise\ don't\ write\ this\ chunk.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02251\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ PNG\_HANDLE\_CHUNK\_NEVER:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02252\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ Do\ not\ write\ the\ chunk.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02253\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ PNG\_HANDLE\_CHUNK\_IF\_SAFE:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02254\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ Write\ the\ chunk\ if\ it\ is\ safe-\/to-\/copy,\ otherwise\ do\ not\ write\ it.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02255\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ PNG\_HANDLE\_CHUNK\_ALWAYS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02256\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ Write\ the\ chunk.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02257\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02258\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Note\ that\ the\ default\ behavior\ is\ effectively\ the\ opposite\ of\ the\ read\ case\ -\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02259\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ in\ read\ unknown\ chunks\ are\ not\ stored\ by\ default,\ in\ write\ they\ are\ written}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02260\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ by\ default.\ \ Also\ the\ behavior\ of\ PNG\_HANDLE\_CHUNK\_IF\_SAFE\ is\ very\ different}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02261\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ -\/\ on\ write\ the\ safe-\/to-\/copy\ bit\ is\ checked,\ on\ read\ the\ critical\ bit\ is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02262\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ checked\ and\ on\ read\ if\ the\ chunk\ is\ critical\ an\ error\ will\ be\ raised.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02263\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02264\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ num\_chunks:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02265\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ ===========}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02266\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ If\ num\_chunks\ is\ positive,\ then\ the\ "{}keep"{}\ parameter\ specifies\ the\ manner}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02267\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ for\ handling\ only\ those\ chunks\ appearing\ in\ the\ chunk\_list\ array,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02268\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ otherwise\ the\ chunk\ list\ array\ is\ ignored.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02269\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02270\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ If\ num\_chunks\ is\ 0\ the\ "{}keep"{}\ parameter\ specifies\ the\ default\ behavior\ for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02271\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ unknown\ chunks,\ as\ described\ above.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02272\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02273\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ If\ num\_chunks\ is\ negative,\ then\ the\ "{}keep"{}\ parameter\ specifies\ the\ manner}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02274\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ for\ handling\ all\ unknown\ chunks\ plus\ all\ chunks\ recognized\ by\ libpng}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02433\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ Interlace\ support.\ \ The\ following\ macros\ are\ always\ defined\ so\ that\ if}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02438\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{02439\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ Two\ macros\ to\ return\ the\ first\ row\ and\ first\ column\ of\ the\ original,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02440\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ full,\ image\ which\ appears\ in\ a\ given\ pass.\ \ 'pass'\ is\ in\ the\ range\ 0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02441\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ to\ 6\ and\ the\ result\ is\ in\ the\ range\ 0\ to\ 7.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02442\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02443\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define\ PNG\_PASS\_START\_ROW(pass)\ (((1\&\string~(pass))<<(3-\/((pass)>>1)))\&7)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02444\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define\ PNG\_PASS\_START\_COL(pass)\ (((1\&\ (pass))<<(3-\/(((pass)+1)>>1)))\&7)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02445\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{02446\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ A\ macro\ to\ return\ the\ offset\ between\ pixels\ in\ the\ output\ row\ for\ a\ pair\ of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02447\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ pixels\ in\ the\ input\ -\/\ effectively\ the\ inverse\ of\ the\ 'COL\_SHIFT'\ macro\ that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02448\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ follows.\ \ Note\ that\ ROW\_OFFSET\ is\ the\ offset\ from\ one\ row\ to\ the\ next\ whereas}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02449\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ COL\_OFFSET\ is\ from\ one\ column\ to\ the\ next,\ within\ a\ row.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02450\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02451\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define\ PNG\_PASS\_ROW\_OFFSET(pass)\ ((pass)>2?(8>>(((pass)-\/1)>>1)):8)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02452\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define\ PNG\_PASS\_COL\_OFFSET(pass)\ (1<<((7-\/(pass))>>1))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02453\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{02454\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ Two\ macros\ to\ help\ evaluate\ the\ number\ of\ rows\ or\ columns\ in\ each}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02455\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ pass.\ \ This\ is\ expressed\ as\ a\ shift\ -\/\ effectively\ log2\ of\ the\ number\ or}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02456\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ rows\ or\ columns\ in\ each\ 8x8\ tile\ of\ the\ original\ image.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02457\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02458\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define\ PNG\_PASS\_ROW\_SHIFT(pass)\ ((pass)>2?(8-\/(pass))>>1:3)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02459\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define\ PNG\_PASS\_COL\_SHIFT(pass)\ ((pass)>1?(7-\/(pass))>>1:3)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02460\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{02461\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ Hence\ two\ macros\ to\ determine\ the\ number\ of\ rows\ or\ columns\ in\ a\ given}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02462\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ pass\ of\ an\ image\ given\ its\ height\ or\ width.\ \ In\ fact\ these\ macros\ may}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02463\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ return\ non-\/zero\ even\ though\ the\ sub-\/image\ is\ empty,\ because\ the\ other}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02464\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ dimension\ may\ be\ empty\ for\ a\ small\ image.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02465\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02466\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define\ PNG\_PASS\_ROWS(height,\ pass)\ (((height)+(((1<<PNG\_PASS\_ROW\_SHIFT(pass))\(\backslash\)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02469\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\ \ \ -\/1)-\/PNG\_PASS\_START\_COL(pass)))>>PNG\_PASS\_COL\_SHIFT(pass))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02470\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{02471\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ For\ the\ reader\ row\ callbacks\ (both\ progressive\ and\ sequential)\ it\ is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02472\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ necessary\ to\ find\ the\ row\ in\ the\ output\ image\ given\ a\ row\ in\ an\ interlaced}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02473\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ image,\ so\ two\ more\ macros:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02474\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02479\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{02480\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ Two\ macros\ which\ return\ a\ boolean\ (0\ or\ 1)\ saying\ whether\ the\ given\ row}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02481\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ or\ column\ is\ in\ a\ particular\ pass.\ \ These\ use\ a\ common\ utility\ macro\ that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02482\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ returns\ a\ mask\ for\ a\ given\ pass\ -\/\ the\ offset\ 'off'\ selects\ the\ row\ or}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02483\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ column\ version.\ \ The\ mask\ has\ the\ appropriate\ bit\ set\ for\ each\ column\ in}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02495\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifdef\ PNG\_READ\_COMPOSITE\_NODIV\_SUPPORTED}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02496\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ With\ these\ routines\ we\ avoid\ an\ integer\ divide,\ which\ will\ be\ slower\ on}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02497\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ most\ machines.\ \ However,\ it\ does\ take\ more\ operations\ than\ the\ corresponding}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02498\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ divide\ method,\ so\ it\ may\ be\ slower\ on\ a\ few\ RISC\ systems.\ \ There\ are\ two}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02499\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ shifts\ (by\ 8\ or\ 16\ bits)\ and\ an\ addition,\ versus\ a\ single\ integer\ divide.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02500\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02501\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Note\ that\ the\ rounding\ factors\ are\ NOT\ supposed\ to\ be\ the\ same!\ \ 128\ and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02502\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ 32768\ are\ correct\ for\ the\ NODIV\ code;\ 127\ and\ 32767\ are\ correct\ for\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02503\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ standard\ method.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02504\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02505\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ [Optimized\ code\ by\ Greg\ Roelofs\ and\ Mark\ Adler...blame\ us\ for\ bugs.\ :-\/)\ ]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02506\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02619\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{02620\ \textcolor{comment}{/*******************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02621\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Section\ 5:\ SIMPLIFIED\ API}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02622\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *******************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02623\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02624\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Please\ read\ the\ documentation\ in\ libpng-\/manual.txt\ (TODO:\ write\ said}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02625\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ documentation)\ if\ you\ don't\ understand\ what\ follows.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02626\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02627\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ The\ simplified\ API\ hides\ the\ details\ of\ both\ libpng\ and\ the\ PNG\ file\ format}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02628\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ itself.\ \ It\ allows\ PNG\ files\ to\ be\ read\ into\ a\ very\ limited\ number\ of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02629\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ in-\/memory\ bitmap\ formats\ or\ to\ be\ written\ from\ the\ same\ formats.\ \ If\ these}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02630\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ formats\ do\ not\ accommodate\ your\ needs\ then\ you\ can,\ and\ should,\ use\ the\ more}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02631\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ sophisticated\ APIs\ above\ -\/\ these\ support\ a\ wide\ variety\ of\ in-\/memory\ formats}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02632\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ and\ a\ wide\ variety\ of\ sophisticated\ transformations\ to\ those\ formats\ as\ well}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02633\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ as\ a\ wide\ variety\ of\ APIs\ to\ manipulate\ ancillary\ information.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02634\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02635\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ To\ read\ a\ PNG\ file\ using\ the\ simplified\ API:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02636\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02637\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ 1)\ Declare\ a\ 'png\_image'\ structure\ (see\ below)\ on\ the\ stack,\ set\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02638\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ version\ field\ to\ PNG\_IMAGE\_VERSION\ and\ the\ 'opaque'\ pointer\ to\ NULL}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02639\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ (this\ is\ REQUIRED,\ your\ program\ may\ crash\ if\ you\ don't\ do\ it.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02640\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ 2)\ Call\ the\ appropriate\ png\_image\_begin\_read...\ function.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02641\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ 3)\ Set\ the\ png\_image\ 'format'\ member\ to\ the\ required\ sample\ format.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02642\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ 4)\ Allocate\ a\ buffer\ for\ the\ image\ and,\ if\ required,\ the\ color-\/map.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02643\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ 5)\ Call\ png\_image\_finish\_read\ to\ read\ the\ image\ and,\ if\ required,\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02644\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ color-\/map\ into\ your\ buffers.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02645\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02646\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ There\ are\ no\ restrictions\ on\ the\ format\ of\ the\ PNG\ input\ itself;\ all\ valid}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02647\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ color\ types,\ bit\ depths,\ and\ interlace\ methods\ are\ acceptable,\ and\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02648\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ input\ image\ is\ transformed\ as\ necessary\ to\ the\ requested\ in-\/memory\ format}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02649\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ during\ the\ png\_image\_finish\_read()\ step.\ \ The\ only\ caveat\ is\ that\ if\ you}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02650\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ request\ a\ color-\/mapped\ image\ from\ a\ PNG\ that\ is\ full-\/color\ or\ makes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02651\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ complex\ use\ of\ an\ alpha\ channel\ the\ transformation\ is\ extremely\ lossy\ and\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02652\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ result\ may\ look\ terrible.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02653\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02654\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ To\ write\ a\ PNG\ file\ using\ the\ simplified\ API:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02655\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02656\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ 1)\ Declare\ a\ 'png\_image'\ structure\ on\ the\ stack\ and\ memset()\ it\ to\ all\ zero.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02657\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ 2)\ Initialize\ the\ members\ of\ the\ structure\ that\ describe\ the\ image,\ setting}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02658\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ the\ 'format'\ member\ to\ the\ format\ of\ the\ image\ samples.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02659\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ 3)\ Call\ the\ appropriate\ png\_image\_write...\ function\ with\ a\ pointer\ to\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02660\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ image\ and,\ if\ necessary,\ the\ color-\/map\ to\ write\ the\ PNG\ data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02661\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02662\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ png\_image\ is\ a\ structure\ that\ describes\ the\ in-\/memory\ format\ of\ an\ image}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02663\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ when\ it\ is\ being\ read\ or\ defines\ the\ in-\/memory\ format\ of\ an\ image\ that\ you}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02664\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ need\ to\ write:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02665\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02666\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if\ defined(PNG\_SIMPLIFIED\_READ\_SUPPORTED)\ ||\ \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02667\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\ \ \ \ defined(PNG\_SIMPLIFIED\_WRITE\_SUPPORTED)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02668\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{02669\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define\ PNG\_IMAGE\_VERSION\ 1}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02683\ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ In\ the\ event\ of\ an\ error\ or\ warning\ the\ following\ field\ will\ be\ set\ to\ a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02684\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ *\ non-\/zero\ value\ and\ the\ 'message'\ field\ will\ contain\ a\ '\(\backslash\)0'\ terminated}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02685\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ *\ string\ with\ the\ libpng\ error\ or\ warning\ message.\ \ If\ both\ warnings\ and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02686\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ *\ an\ error\ were\ encountered,\ only\ the\ error\ is\ recorded.\ \ If\ there}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02688\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ *}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02690\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ *\ a\ value\ as\ follows:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02691\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02692\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#\ \ define\ PNG\_IMAGE\_WARNING\ 1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02693\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#\ \ define\ PNG\_IMAGE\_ERROR\ 2}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02694\ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02695\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ *\ The\ result\ is\ a\ two-\/bit\ code\ such\ that\ a\ value\ more\ than\ 1\ indicates}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02696\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ *\ a\ failure\ in\ the\ API\ just\ called:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02697\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02698\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ *\ \ \ \ 0\ -\/\ no\ warning\ or\ error}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02699\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ *\ \ \ \ 1\ -\/\ warning}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02700\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ *\ \ \ \ 2\ -\/\ error}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02701\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ *\ \ \ \ 3\ -\/\ error\ preceded\ by\ warning}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02706\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{02707\ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ message[64];}
\DoxyCodeLine{02708\ \}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{structpng__image}{png\_image}},\ *\mbox{\hyperlink{libpng16_2png_8h_a849cd575ed0f106df40172e07d04c0f8}{png\_imagep}};}
\DoxyCodeLine{02709\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{02710\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ The\ samples\ of\ the\ image\ have\ one\ to\ four\ channels\ whose\ components\ have}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02711\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ original\ values\ in\ the\ range\ 0\ to\ 1.0:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02712\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02713\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ 1:\ A\ single\ gray\ or\ luminance\ channel\ (G).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02714\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ 2:\ A\ gray/luminance\ channel\ and\ an\ alpha\ channel\ (GA).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02715\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ 3:\ Three\ red,\ green,\ blue\ color\ channels\ (RGB).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02716\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ 4:\ Three\ color\ channels\ and\ an\ alpha\ channel\ (RGBA).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02717\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02718\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ The\ components\ are\ encoded\ in\ one\ of\ two\ ways:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02719\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02720\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ a)\ As\ a\ small\ integer,\ value\ 0..255,\ contained\ in\ a\ single\ byte.\ \ For\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02721\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ alpha\ channel\ the\ original\ value\ is\ simply\ value/255.\ \ For\ the\ color\ or}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02722\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ luminance\ channels\ the\ value\ is\ encoded\ according\ to\ the\ sRGB\ specification}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02723\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ and\ matches\ the\ 8-\/bit\ format\ expected\ by\ typical\ display\ devices.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02724\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02725\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ The\ color/gray\ channels\ are\ not\ scaled\ (pre-\/multiplied)\ by\ the\ alpha}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02726\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ channel\ and\ are\ suitable\ for\ passing\ to\ color\ management\ software.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02727\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02728\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ b)\ As\ a\ value\ in\ the\ range\ 0..65535,\ contained\ in\ a\ 2-\/byte\ integer.\ \ All}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02729\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ channels\ can\ be\ converted\ to\ the\ original\ value\ by\ dividing\ by\ 65535;\ all}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02730\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ channels\ are\ linear.\ \ Color\ channels\ use\ the\ RGB\ encoding\ (RGB\ end-\/points)\ of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02731\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ the\ sRGB\ specification.\ \ This\ encoding\ is\ identified\ by\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02732\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ PNG\_FORMAT\_FLAG\_LINEAR\ flag\ below.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02733\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02734\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ When\ the\ simplified\ API\ needs\ to\ convert\ between\ sRGB\ and\ linear\ colorspaces,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02735\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ the\ actual\ sRGB\ transfer\ curve\ defined\ in\ the\ sRGB\ specification\ (see\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02736\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ article\ at\ <https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/SRGB>)\ is\ used,\ not\ the\ gamma=1/2.2}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02737\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ approximation\ used\ elsewhere\ in\ libpng.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02738\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02739\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ When\ an\ alpha\ channel\ is\ present\ it\ is\ expected\ to\ denote\ pixel\ coverage}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02740\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ of\ the\ color\ or\ luminance\ channels\ and\ is\ returned\ as\ an\ associated\ alpha}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02741\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ channel:\ the\ color/gray\ channels\ are\ scaled\ (pre-\/multiplied)\ by\ the\ alpha}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02742\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ value.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02743\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02744\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ The\ samples\ are\ either\ contained\ directly\ in\ the\ image\ data,\ between\ 1\ and\ 8}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02745\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ bytes\ per\ pixel\ according\ to\ the\ encoding,\ or\ are\ held\ in\ a\ color-\/map\ indexed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02746\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ by\ bytes\ in\ the\ image\ data.\ \ In\ the\ case\ of\ a\ color-\/map\ the\ color-\/map\ entries}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02747\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ are\ individual\ samples,\ encoded\ as\ above,\ and\ the\ image\ data\ has\ one\ byte\ per}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02748\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ pixel\ to\ select\ the\ relevant\ sample\ from\ the\ color-\/map.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02749\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02750\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{02751\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ PNG\_FORMAT\_*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02752\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02753\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \#defines\ to\ be\ used\ in\ png\_image::format.\ \ Each\ \#define\ identifies\ a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02754\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ particular\ layout\ of\ sample\ data\ and,\ if\ present,\ alpha\ values.\ \ There\ are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02755\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ separate\ defines\ for\ each\ of\ the\ two\ component\ encodings.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02756\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02757\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ A\ format\ is\ built\ up\ using\ single\ bit\ flag\ values.\ \ All\ combinations\ are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02758\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ valid.\ \ Formats\ can\ be\ built\ up\ from\ the\ flag\ values\ or\ you\ can\ use\ one\ of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02759\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ the\ predefined\ values\ below.\ \ When\ testing\ formats\ always\ use\ the\ FORMAT\_FLAG}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02760\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ macros\ to\ test\ for\ individual\ features\ -\/\ future\ versions\ of\ the\ library\ may}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02761\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ add\ new\ flags.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02762\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02763\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ When\ reading\ or\ writing\ color-\/mapped\ images\ the\ format\ should\ be\ set\ to\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02764\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ format\ of\ the\ entries\ in\ the\ color-\/map\ then\ png\_image\_\{read,write\}\_colormap}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02765\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ called\ to\ read\ or\ write\ the\ color-\/map\ and\ set\ the\ format\ correctly\ for\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02766\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ image\ data.\ \ Do\ not\ set\ the\ PNG\_FORMAT\_FLAG\_COLORMAP\ bit\ directly!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02767\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02768\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ NOTE:\ libpng\ can\ be\ built\ with\ particular\ features\ disabled.\ If\ you\ see}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02769\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ compiler\ errors\ because\ the\ definition\ of\ one\ of\ the\ following\ flags\ has\ been}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02770\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ compiled\ out\ it\ is\ because\ libpng\ does\ not\ have\ the\ required\ support.\ \ It\ is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02771\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ possible,\ however,\ for\ the\ libpng\ configuration\ to\ enable\ the\ format\ on\ just}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02772\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ read\ or\ just\ write;\ in\ that\ case\ you\ may\ see\ an\ error\ at\ run\ time.\ \ You\ can}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02773\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ guard\ against\ this\ by\ checking\ for\ the\ definition\ of\ the\ appropriate}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02774\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ "{}\_SUPPORTED"{}\ macro,\ one\ of:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02775\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02776\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ PNG\_SIMPLIFIED\_\{READ,WRITE\}\_\{BGR,AFIRST\}\_SUPPORTED}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02777\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02778\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define\ PNG\_FORMAT\_FLAG\_ALPHA\ \ \ \ 0x01U\ }\textcolor{comment}{/*\ format\ with\ an\ alpha\ channel\ */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02779\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define\ PNG\_FORMAT\_FLAG\_COLOR\ \ \ \ 0x02U\ }\textcolor{comment}{/*\ color\ format:\ otherwise\ grayscale\ */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02780\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define\ PNG\_FORMAT\_FLAG\_LINEAR\ \ \ 0x04U\ }\textcolor{comment}{/*\ 2-\/byte\ channels\ else\ 1-\/byte\ */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02781\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define\ PNG\_FORMAT\_FLAG\_COLORMAP\ 0x08U\ }\textcolor{comment}{/*\ image\ data\ is\ color-\/mapped\ */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02782\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{02783\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifdef\ PNG\_FORMAT\_BGR\_SUPPORTED}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02784\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#\ \ define\ PNG\_FORMAT\_FLAG\_BGR\ \ \ \ 0x10U\ }\textcolor{comment}{/*\ BGR\ colors,\ else\ order\ is\ RGB\ */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02785\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02786\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{02787\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifdef\ PNG\_FORMAT\_AFIRST\_SUPPORTED}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02788\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#\ \ define\ PNG\_FORMAT\_FLAG\_AFIRST\ 0x20U\ }\textcolor{comment}{/*\ alpha\ channel\ comes\ first\ */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02789\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02790\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{02791\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define\ PNG\_FORMAT\_FLAG\_ASSOCIATED\_ALPHA\ 0x40U\ }\textcolor{comment}{/*\ alpha\ channel\ is\ associated\ */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02792\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{02793\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ Commonly\ used\ formats\ have\ predefined\ macros.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02794\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02795\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ First\ the\ single\ byte\ (sRGB)\ formats:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02796\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02797\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define\ PNG\_FORMAT\_GRAY\ 0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02798\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define\ PNG\_FORMAT\_GA\ \ \ PNG\_FORMAT\_FLAG\_ALPHA}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02806\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{02807\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ Then\ the\ linear\ 2-\/byte\ formats.\ \ When\ naming\ these\ "{}Y"{}\ is\ used\ to}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02809\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02810\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define\ PNG\_FORMAT\_LINEAR\_Y\ PNG\_FORMAT\_FLAG\_LINEAR}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02815\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{02816\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ With\ color-\/mapped\ formats\ the\ image\ data\ is\ one\ byte\ for\ each\ pixel,\ the\ byte}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02817\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ is\ an\ index\ into\ the\ color-\/map\ which\ is\ formatted\ as\ above.\ \ To\ obtain\ a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02818\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ color-\/mapped\ format\ it\ is\ sufficient\ just\ to\ add\ the\ PNG\_FOMAT\_FLAG\_COLORMAP}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02820\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02822\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define\ PNG\_FORMAT\_BGR\_COLORMAP\ \ (PNG\_FORMAT\_BGR|PNG\_FORMAT\_FLAG\_COLORMAP)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02827\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{02828\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ PNG\_IMAGE\ macros}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02829\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02830\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ These\ are\ convenience\ macros\ to\ derive\ information\ from\ a\ png\_image}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02831\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ structure.\ \ The\ PNG\_IMAGE\_SAMPLE\_\ macros\ return\ values\ appropriate\ to\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02832\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ actual\ image\ sample\ values\ -\/\ either\ the\ entries\ in\ the\ color-\/map\ or\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02833\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ pixels\ in\ the\ image.\ \ The\ PNG\_IMAGE\_PIXEL\_\ macros\ return\ corresponding\ values}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02834\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ for\ the\ pixels\ and\ will\ always\ return\ 1\ for\ color-\/mapped\ formats.\ \ The}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02835\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ remaining\ macros\ return\ information\ about\ the\ rows\ in\ the\ image\ and\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02836\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ complete\ image.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02837\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02838\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ NOTE:\ All\ the\ macros\ that\ take\ a\ png\_image::format\ parameter\ are\ compile\ time}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02839\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ constants\ if\ the\ format\ parameter\ is,\ itself,\ a\ constant.\ \ Therefore\ these}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02840\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ macros\ can\ be\ used\ in\ array\ declarations\ and\ case\ labels\ where\ required.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02841\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Similarly\ the\ macros\ are\ also\ pre-\/processor\ constants\ (sizeof\ is\ not\ used)\ so}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02842\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ they\ can\ be\ used\ in\ \#if\ tests.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02843\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02844\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ First\ the\ information\ about\ the\ samples.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02845\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02846\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define\ PNG\_IMAGE\_SAMPLE\_CHANNELS(fmt)\(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02847\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\ \ \ (((fmt)\&(PNG\_FORMAT\_FLAG\_COLOR|PNG\_FORMAT\_FLAG\_ALPHA))+1)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02848\ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ Return\ the\ total\ number\ of\ channels\ in\ a\ given\ format:\ 1..4\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02849\ }

\DoxyCodeLine{02862\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{02863\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define\ PNG\_IMAGE\_MAXIMUM\_COLORMAP\_COMPONENTS(fmt)\(\backslash\)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02903\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ *\ row.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02904\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ *}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02909\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{02910\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define\ PNG\_IMAGE\_BUFFER\_SIZE(image,\ row\_stride)\(\backslash\)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02913\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ *\ stride\ -\/\ the\ number\ of\ components\ to\ leave\ space\ for\ in\ each\ row.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02914\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02915\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ *\ WARNING:\ this\ macro\ overflows\ a\ 32-\/bit\ integer\ for\ some\ large\ PNG\ images,}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02917\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02927\ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ Return\ the\ size,\ in\ bytes,\ of\ the\ color-\/map\ of\ this\ image.\ \ If\ the\ image}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02928\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ *\ format\ is\ not\ a\ color-\/map\ format\ this\ will\ return\ a\ size\ sufficient\ for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02929\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ *\ 256\ entries\ in\ the\ given\ format;\ check\ PNG\_FORMAT\_FLAG\_COLORMAP\ if}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02930\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ *\ you\ don't\ want\ to\ allocate\ a\ color-\/map\ in\ this\ case.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02931\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02932\ }

\DoxyCodeLine{03124\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{03125\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ You\ can\ pre-\/allocate\ the\ buffer\ by\ making\ sure\ it\ is\ of\ sufficient\ size}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03126\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ regardless\ of\ the\ amount\ of\ compression\ achieved.\ \ The\ buffer\ size\ will}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03127\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ always\ be\ bigger\ than\ the\ original\ image\ and\ it\ will\ never\ be\ filled.\ \ The}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03128\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ following\ macros\ are\ provided\ to\ assist\ in\ allocating\ the\ buffer.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03129\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03130\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define\ PNG\_IMAGE\_DATA\_SIZE(image)\ (PNG\_IMAGE\_SIZE(image)+(image).height)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03131\ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ The\ number\ of\ uncompressed\ bytes\ in\ the\ PNG\ byte\ encoding\ of\ the\ image;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03132\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ *\ uncompressing\ the\ PNG\ IDAT\ data\ will\ give\ this\ number\ of\ bytes.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03133\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03134\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ *\ NOTE:\ while\ PNG\_IMAGE\_SIZE\ cannot\ overflow\ for\ an\ image\ in\ memory\ this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03135\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ *\ macro\ can\ because\ of\ the\ extra\ bytes\ used\ in\ the\ PNG\ byte\ encoding.\ \ You}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03136\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ *\ need\ to\ avoid\ this\ macro\ if\ your\ image\ size\ approaches\ 2\string^30\ in\ width\ or}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03137\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ *\ height.\ \ The\ same\ goes\ for\ the\ remainder\ of\ these\ macros;\ they\ all\ produce}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03138\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ *\ bigger\ numbers\ than\ the\ actual\ in-\/memory\ image\ size.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03139\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03140\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifndef\ PNG\_ZLIB\_MAX\_SIZE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03141\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#\ \ define\ PNG\_ZLIB\_MAX\_SIZE(b)\ ((b)+(((b)+7U)>>3)+(((b)+63U)>>6)+11U)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03142\ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ An\ upper\ bound\ on\ the\ number\ of\ compressed\ bytes\ given\ 'b'\ uncompressed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03143\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ *\ bytes.\ \ This\ is\ based\ on\ deflateBounds()\ in\ zlib;\ different}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03144\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ *\ implementations\ of\ zlib\ compression\ may\ conceivably\ produce\ more\ data\ so}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03145\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ *\ if\ your\ zlib\ implementation\ is\ not\ zlib\ itself\ redefine\ this\ macro}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03146\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ *\ appropriately.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03147\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03148\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03149\ }

\DoxyCodeLine{03152\ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ An\ upper\ bound\ on\ the\ size\ of\ the\ data\ in\ the\ PNG\ IDAT\ chunks.\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03153\ }

\DoxyCodeLine{03181\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Section\ 6:\ IMPLEMENTATION\ OPTIONS}}

\DoxyCodeLine{03183\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03184\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Support\ for\ arbitrary\ implementation-\/specific\ optimizations.\ \ The\ API\ allows}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03185\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ particular\ options\ to\ be\ turned\ on\ or\ off.\ \ 'Option'\ is\ the\ number\ of\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03186\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ option\ and\ 'onoff'\ is\ 0\ (off)\ or\ non-\/0\ (on).\ \ The\ value\ returned\ is\ given}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03187\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ by\ the\ PNG\_OPTION\_\ defines\ below.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03188\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03189\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ HARDWARE:\ normally\ hardware\ capabilities,\ such\ as\ the\ Intel\ SSE\ instructions,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03190\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ are\ detected\ at\ run\ time,\ however\ sometimes\ it\ may\ be\ impossible}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03191\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ to\ do\ this\ in\ user\ mode,\ in\ which\ case\ it\ is\ necessary\ to\ discover}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03192\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ the\ capabilities\ in\ an\ OS\ specific\ way.\ \ Such\ capabilities\ are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03193\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ listed\ here\ when\ libpng\ has\ support\ for\ them\ and\ must\ be\ turned}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03194\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ ON\ by\ the\ application\ if\ present.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03195\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03196\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ SOFTWARE:\ sometimes\ software\ optimizations\ actually\ result\ in\ performance}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03197\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ decrease\ on\ some\ architectures\ or\ systems,\ or\ with\ some\ sets\ of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03198\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ PNG\ images.\ \ 'Software'\ options\ allow\ such\ optimizations\ to\ be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03199\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ selected\ at\ run\ time.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03200\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}
